 is act kaa upbandh 51 or 52 aise hai, jinke baad farji doctoron kii baadh aa jaaegi, jisase jan swasthya bhi prabhavit hoga
 The Union Cabinet approved the bill on 17 July
 vidheyak kaa mukhya uddeshy medical council of india (emsiai) ke sthaan par ek chikitsa ayog sthapit karnaa he
 It is said that this will repeal the Indian Medical Council Act 1956
 chikitsa ayog nijee medical collejon or dimd vishvavidhyalayon main 50 fisadi siton ke liye sabhi shulkon kaa niyaman karegaa
 Which is expected to reduce the entry fee

 While doctors object to this because it will endanger the lives of patients
